# Daily Work Log

Use this file for daily engineering knowledge capture.

## Entry format

- Date: `YYYY-MM-DD`
- Summary: What was changed/fixed/decided
- Files touched: Comma-separated paths (or `none`)
- Validation: Lint/tests/manual check status
- Notes/risks: Optional follow-up items

| 2026-03-10 | Confirmed the live gift-certificate redemption rule for `dbRetailer_SS2018` and updated the shared migration assets accordingly. Read-only legacy code review plus MSSQL stored-procedure inspection showed that `frmInvoice_GST` scans gift coupons as `GV/GU-YYYYmm-VoucherNo-LineId`, `Select_GiftCouponDetails` returns `GiftCouponH.CouponValue`, and invoice save persists only `F_GiftCouponH/F_GiftCouponL`. Based on that, the retail templates and runbook now treat `GiftCouponL.Id` as the real certificate key for this client, add a line-level `CRM_GIFT_CERTIFICATES_QUERY`, and define redemption import as full `GiftCouponH.CouponValue` per linked line. | `backend/scripts/mssql-import/retail-crm-barcode-query-templates.sql`, `backend/scripts/mssql-import/crm-barcode-common-map.yml`, `docs/runbooks/retail_mssql_crm_barcode_migration_framework.md`, `docs/knowledge-book/daily-work-log.md` | Live read-only MSSQL validation was rerun against `dbRetailer_SS2018` on `DESKTOP-6C1LQA8:52583` with the Node `mssql` driver, including stored-procedure definition reads for `Select_GiftCouponDetails` and `Insert_Update_InvoiceH` plus line-level usage counts (`6,627` total lines, `176` redeemed, `3,441` active unused, `3,010` cancelled).
